I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT: 0.877·P·sin(0.567·t) + 0.701·(1 - P/65.75)·P**

So GT = c_a·P·sin(c_b·t) + c_c·P + c_d·P²

where c_a = 0.877, c_b = 0.567, c_c = 0.701, c_d = -0.01066

The GT has three basis function components: **P·sin(ωt)**, **P**, and **P²**.

Let me check each candidate:

### Candidate 1:

### Candidate 2:
